<script >
    /* global Bigpipe */
    (function() {
        "use strict";
        Bigpipe.addEventListener('beforepageletload', function (pagelet) {
            // pagelet每次接受到子pagelet的emit都更新当前加载时间

            pagelet.on('styleloaded', function () {
                this.dpStyleLoadedTime = +new Date;
            });
            pagelet.on('scriptloaded', function () {
                this.dpScriptLoadedTime = +new Date;
            });
        });
        Bigpipe.addEventListener('pageletstyleloaded', function (pagelet) {
            pagelet.emit('styleloaded');
            this.dpSelfStyleLoadedTime = +new Date;
        });
        Bigpipe.addEventListener('pageletscriptloaded', function (pagelet) {
            pagelet.emit('scriptloaded');
            this.dpSelfScriptLoadedTime = +new Date;
        });
        Bigpipe.addEventListener('pageloaded', function (pagelets) {
            // 关键pagelet及统计字段
            // todo frs_head 和 search_pagelet 改名!!!!!
            var targetPagelet = [
                {
                    name: 'frs-header/pagelet/head',
                    showKey: 'c_head_pagelet_show',
                    loadedKey: 'c_head_pagelet_loaded'
                },
                {
                    name: 'search/pagelet/search_logic',
                    showKey: 'c_search_pagelet_show',
                    loadedKey: 'c_search_pagelet_loaded'
                },
                {
                    name: 'frs-list/pagelet/content',
                    showKey: 'c_list_pagelet_show',
                    loadedKey: 'c_list_pagelet_loaded'
                },
                {
                    name: 'frs-aside/pagelet/aside',
                    showKey: 'c_aside_pagelet_show',
                    loadedKey: 'c_aside_pagelet_loaded'
                },
                {
                    name: 'frs-footer/pagelet/content_footer',
                    showKey: 'c_foot_pagelet_show',
                    loadedKey: 'c_foot_pagelet_loaded'
                }
            ];

            var minShowTime;
            var minLoadedTime;
            var maxShowTime;

            $.each(targetPagelet, function () {
                var pagelet = pagelets[this.name];
                if (pagelet && alog && alog.fire) {
                    alog('speed.set', this.showKey, this.isSelf ? pagelet.dpSelfStyleLoadedTime : pagelet.dpStyleLoadedTime);
                    alog.fire("mark");
                    alog('speed.set', this.loadedKey, this.isSelf ? pagelet.dpSelfScriptLoadedTime : pagelet.dpScriptLoadedTime);
                    alog.fire("mark");
                    // 取style加载时间的最小值
                    minShowTime = (!minShowTime || minShowTime > pagelet.dpStyleLoadedTime) ? pagelet.dpStyleLoadedTime : minShowTime;
                    // 取script加载时间的最小值
                    minLoadedTime = (!minLoadedTime || minLoadedTime > pagelet.dpScriptLoadedTime) ? pagelet.dpScriptLoadedTime : minLoadedTime;
                    // 取style加载时间的最大值
                    maxShowTime = (!maxShowTime || maxShowTime < pagelet.dpStyleLoadedTime) ? pagelet.dpStyleLoadedTime : maxShowTime;
                }
            });

            // 记录第一个pagelet的展现和总加载时间
            if (minShowTime && minLoadedTime) {
                alog('speed.set', 'c_first_pagelet_show', minShowTime);
                alog.fire("mark");
                alog('speed.set', 'c_first_pagelet_loaded', minLoadedTime);
                alog.fire("mark");
            }
            // dom ready time，这里定义是所有pagelets的style loaded时间
            alog('speed.set', 'drt', maxShowTime);
        });
    })();

                $post.slideUp();
                $talk.slideUp();
                $(this).removeClass('down');
                interview.stop();
            }else{
                if(!$post.hasClass('onlyPost')){
                    $talk.slideDown();
                }
                $post.slideDown();
                $editor.slideDown();
                $(this).addClass('down');
                interview.start();
            }
        });

        if(!atInfo)return;
        if(atInfo.isAladdin){
            if(atInfo.uname=='aladdiniframe') {
                interview.scroll2top( $("#threadListGroupCnt") );
            }else{
                if (Boolean("")) {
                    interview.$editorHolder.trigger("click.focus");
                    interview.scroll2editor(215);
                }else{
                    interview.scroll2editor( 200 );
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        interview.shakeEditorBorder();
                    }, 400);
                }
                if(atInfo.uname != null){
                    if(atInfo.pid != null){
                        setTimeout(function(){
                            interview.editor.trigger('atSomeOne', atInfo);
                        }, 200);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>
